the\\n109: \\t// Endpoints object change.\\n110: \\t//\\n111: \\t// Given the definition of the \\\"endpoints change trigger\\\", please note that this annotation will\\n112: \\t// be set ONLY for \\t// in the Annotations of a Node.\\n70: \\tPreferAvoidPodsAnnotationKey string = \\\"scheduler.alpha.kubernetes.io/preferAvoidPods\\\"\\n71: \\n72: \\t// ObjectTTLAnnotationKey represents a \\t//\\n88: \\t// It should be a comma-separated list of CIDRs, e.g. `0.0.0.0/0` to\\n89: \\t// allow full access (the default) or `18.0.0.0/8,56.0.0.0/8` to allow\\n90: \\t// access only from the timestamp (stored as RFC 3339 date-time string, e.g. '2018-10-22T19:32:52.1Z')\\n97: \\t// of the last change, of some Pod or Service object, that triggered the endpoints object change.\\n98: \\t// In other words, if a Pod / Service changed at time T0, that change was observed by endpoints\\n99: \\t// controller at T1, and the Endpoints object was changed at T2, the\\n100: \\t// EndpointsLastChangeTriggerTime would be set to T0.\\n101: \\t//\\n102: \\t// The \\\"endpoints change trigger\\\" here means any Pod or Service change that resulted in the\\n103: \\t// Endpoints object change.\\n104: \\t//\\n105: \\t// Given the definition of the \\\"endpoints change trigger\\\", please note that this annotation will\\n106: \\t// be set ONLY for endpoints object changes triggered by either Pod or Service change. If the\\n107: \\t// Endpoints object changes due to other reasons, this annotation won't be set (or updated if it's\\n108: \\t// already set).\\n109: \\t//\\n110: \\t// This annotation will be used to compute the in-cluster network programming latency SLI, see\\n111: \\t// https://github.com/kubernetes/community/blob/master/sig-scalability/slos/network_programming_latency.md\\n112: \\tEndpointsLastChangeTriggerTime = \\\"endpoints.kubernetes.io/last-change-trigger-time\\\"\\n113: \\n114: \\t// EndpointsOverCapacity will be set on an Endpoints resource when it\\n115: \\t// exceeds the maximum capacity of 1000 addresses. Pods with lower\\n130: \\t// deletion cost are preferred to be deleted before pods with higher deletion cost.\\n131: \\t// Note that this is honored on a best-effort basis, and so it does not offer guarantees on\\n132: \\t// pod deletion order.\\n133: \\t// The implicit deletion cost for pods that don't set the annotation is 0, negative values are permitted.\\n134: \\t//\\n135: \\t// This annotation is beta-level and is only honored when PodDeletionCost feature is enabled.\\n136: \\tPodDeletionCost = \\\"controller.kubernetes.io/pod-deletion-cost\\\"\\n137: \\n138: \\t// DeprecatedAnnotationTopologyAwareHints can be used to enable or disable\\n139: \\t// Topology Aware Hints for a Service. This may be set to \\\"Auto\\\" or\\n140: \\t// \\\"Disabled\\\". Any other value is treated as \\\"Disabled\\\". This annotation has\\n141: \\t// been deprecated in favor of the `service.kubernetes.io/topology-mode`\\n142: \\t// annotation which also allows \\\"Auto\\\" and \\\"Disabled\\\", but is not limited to\\n143: \\t// those (it's open ended to provide room for experimentation while we\\n144: \\t// pursue configuration for topology via specification). When both\\n145: \\t// `service.kubernetes.io/topology-aware-hints` and\\n146: \\t// `service.kubernetes.io/topology-mode` annotations are set, the value of\\n147: \\t// `service.kubernetes.io/topology-aware-hints` has precedence.\\n148: \\tDeprecatedAnnotationTopologyAwareHints = \\\"service.kubernetes.io/topology-aware-hints\\\"\\n149: \\n150: \\t// AnnotationTopologyMode can be used to enable or disable Topology Aware\\n151: \\t// Routing for a Service. Well known values are \\\"Auto\\\" and \\\"Disabled\\\".\\n152: \\t// Implementations may choose to develop new topology approaches, exposing\\n153: \\t// them with domain-prefixed values. For example, \\\"example.com/lowest-rtt\\\"\\n154: \\t// could be a valid implementation-specific value for this annotation. These\\n155: \\t// heuristics will often populate topology hints on EndpointSlices, but that\\n156: \\t// is not a requirement.\\n157: \\tAnnotationTopologyMode = \\\"service.kubernetes.io/topology-mode\\\"\\n158: )\\n159: endpoints\n99: \t// controller at T1, and the Endpoints object was changed at T2, the\n100: \t// EndpointsLastChangeTriggerTime would be set to T0.\n101: \t//\n102: \t// The \"endpoints change trigger\" here means any Pod or Service change that resulted in the\n103: \t// Endpoints object change.\n104: \t//\n105: \t// Given the definition of the \"endpoints change trigger\", please note that this annotation will\n106: \t// be set ONLY for endpoints object changes triggered by either Pod or Service change. If the\n107: \t// Endpoints object changes due to other reasons, this annotation won't be set (or updated if it's\n108: \t// already set).\n109: \t//\n110: \t// This annotation will be used to compute the in-cluster network programming latency SLI, see\n111: \t// https://github.com/kubernetes/community/blob/master/sig-scalability/slos/network_programming_latency.md\n112: \tEndpointsLastChangeTriggerTime = \"endpoints.kubernetes.io/last-change-trigger-time\"\n113: \n114: \t// EndpointsOverCapacity will be set on an Endpoints resource when it\n115: \t// exceeds the maximum capacity of 1000 addresses. Initially the Endpoints\n116: \t// controller will set this annotation with a value of \"warning\". In a\n117: \t// future release, the controller may set this annotation with a value of\n118: \t// \"truncated\" to indicate that any addresses exceeding the limit of 1000\n119: \t// have been truncated from the Endpoints resource.\n120: \tEndpointsOverCapacity = \"endpoints.kubernetes.io/over-capacity\"\n121: \n122: \t// MigratedPluginsAnnotationKey is the annotation key, set for CSINode objects, that is a comma-separated\n123: \t// list of in-tree plugins that will be serviced by the CSI backend on the Node represented by CSINode.\n124: \t// This annotation is used by the Attach Detach Controller to determine whether to use the in-tree or\n125: \t// CSI Backend for a volume plugin on a specific node.\n126: \tMigratedPluginsAnnotationKey = \"storage.alpha.kubernetes.io/migrated-plugins\"\n127: \n128: \t// PodDeletionCost can be used to set to an int32 that represent the cost of deleting\n129: \t// a pod compared to other pods belonging to the same ReplicaSet. Pods with lower\n130: \t// deletion cost are preferred to be deleted before pods with higher deletion cost.\n131: \t// Note that this is honored on a best-effort basis, and so it does not offer guarantees on\n132: \t// pod deletion order.\n133: \t// The implicit deletion cost for pods that don't set the annotation is 0, negative values are permitted.\n134: \t//\n135: \t// This annotation is beta-level and is only honored when PodDeletionCost feature is enabled.\n136: \tPodDeletionCost = \"controller.kubernetes.io/pod-deletion-cost\"\n137: \n138: \t// DeprecatedAnnotationTopologyAwareHints can be used to enable or disable\n139: \t// Topology Aware Hints for a Service. This may be set to \"Auto\" or\n140: \t// \"Disabled\". Any other value is treated as \"Disabled\". This annotation has\n141: \t// been deprecated in favor of the `service.kubernetes.io/topology-mode`\n142: \t// annotation which also allows \"Auto\" and \"Disabled\", but is not limited to\n143: \t// those (it's open ended to provide room for experimentation while we\n144: \t// pursue configuration for topology via specification). When both\n145: \t// `service.kubernetes.io/topology-aware-hints` and\n146: \t// `service.kubernetes.io/topology-mode` annotations are set, the value of\n147: \t// `service.kubernetes.io/topology-aware-hints` has precedence.\n148: \tDeprecatedAnnotationTopologyAwareHints = \"service.kubernetes.io/topology-aware-hints\"\n149: \n150: \t// AnnotationTopologyMode can be used to enable or disable Topology Aware\n151: \t// Routing for a Service. Well known values are \"Auto\" and \"Disabled\".\n152: \t// Implementations may choose to develop new topology approaches, exposing\n153: \t// them with domain-prefixed values. For example, \"example.com/lowest-rtt\"\n154: \t// could be a valid implementation-specific value for this annotation. These\n155: \t// heuristics will often populate topology hints on EndpointSlices, but that\n156: \t// is not a requirement.\n157: \tAnnotationTopologyMode = \"service.kubernetes.io/topology-mode\"\n158: )\n159: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes@cc415b71c5f2cc8ea30f2574c7124b06a9f1b78c/-/blob/pkg/apis/core/annotation_key_constants.go"}}}
